### [1] [GeoISF: Instance Semantic Forest Inspired Large-Scale Cross-View Geo-Localization via Ground LiDAR-to-Satellite Image](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28371)
*Di Hu,Xia Yuan,Chunxia Zhao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出GeoISF：利用基于WordNet的“实例语义森林”将多帧LiDAR语义整合为共享环境表示，从而跨模态（点云-卫星图像）在大尺度场景中实现高精度定位；在KITTI上R@10较并行方法提升13.22倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大尺度跨视角定位中，LiDAR点云与卫星图像存在显著模态差异与语义对齐不足，现有方法在大范围检索下召回率与计算代价不理想，缺乏稳健的语义桥接与时序信息整合机制。

Method: 构建GeoISF管线：1）以WordNet为先验构建“实例语义森林”，将多帧点云的语义树融合，形成时间上一致且可判别的环境语义表示；2）以该共享语义中介对齐LiDAR与卫星图像特征，提升跨模态匹配；3）在大范围候选库上进行高效检索与匹配评估。

Result: 在KITTI等大尺度基准上进行广泛实验，GeoISF在R@10指标上相较并行的LiDAR-to-image方法实现13.22倍提升，表现出更高的语义匹配精度与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: GeoISF通过语义森林统一跨模态表示与多帧时序信息，显著改善大尺度LiDAR-卫星图像定位的准确性与效率，弥补现有方法在大场景中的性能缺口；代码将开源，便于社区复现与扩展。

Abstract: The problem of localization on a large-scale satellite image given a frame of query ground view point clouds remains challenging. Existing LiDAR-to-image cross-view localization methods struggle in large-scale scenarios due to limited semantic alignment and the modality gap between point clouds and satellite images. This paper introduces the large-scale LiDAR-to-image geo-localization pipeline called GeoISF. GeoISF introduces an instance semantic forest constructed using WordNet, which enhances temporal semantic representation and discriminative power by integrating semantic trees from multiple frames. By leveraging environmental semantic representation as a shared medium, GeoISF effectively bridges the modality gap and improves semantic matching accuracy. Extensive experiments demonstrate the superior performance of GeoISF in large-scale cross-view localization, 13.22 times better than the parallel LiDAR-to-image method in the R@10 metric on the KITTI dataset. The proposed method addresses the existing gap in large-scale LiDAR-to-image cross-view localization, offering a robust solution to the computational and accuracy challenges inherent in such scenarios. We will release the code as an open-source resource available online for the broader research community.

</details>


### [2] [Memory-Augmented LSTM Autoencoder for Unsupervised Activity Recognition with IMU Sensor Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28377)
*Saeid Arabzadeh,Farshad Almasganj,Mohammad Mahdi Ahmadi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种完全无监督的时空特征融合框架（记忆增强自编码器）用于IMU人体活动识别，在短时间窗、现实分割设置下于DaLiAc和PAMAP2获96.6%/98.4%准确率，超越监督与无监督基线，并显著提升可分性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有HAR依赖大量标注、传感器多源融合复杂，且无监督方法难以捕获时空依赖；真实环境中噪声、活动重叠、缺失标签使问题更严峻。因此需在短时间窗、无标签条件下实现鲁棒的多传感器时空特征学习。

Method: 构建记忆增强的自编码框架：1) 用堆叠自编码器从多IMU通道提取层级静态特征，并在传感器内与跨传感器进行融合；2) 采用序列到序列LSTM自编码器进行时间建模与历史模式整合，无需标签；3) 系统化调参以在短窗约束下最大化特征可分性；4) 采用更贴近现实的“跨类别窗口”分割评估。

Result: 在DaLiAc与PAMAP2数据集上，使用现实的跨类窗口分割仍取得96.6%与98.4%准确率，超过监督基线与无监督对手；短窗下特征可分性提升最高达9%；现实分割带来约7%的准确率下降但更具实际意义。

Conclusion: 无监督、记忆增强的时空特征融合在短窗与现实分割条件下实现强鲁棒性与高准确率，可作为实时医疗监测与康复的实用方案，减少标注依赖与复杂融合代价，同时更好反映真实活动过渡。

Abstract: HAR using Inertial Measurement Unit (IMU) sensors is vital for healthcare monitoring and rehabilitation. Despite deep learning advancements, major challenges remain: reliance on labeled data, multi-sensor fusion complexity, and the limited ability of unsupervised methods to capture spatiotemporal dependencies. These issues are pronounced in real-world scenarios with noisy data, overlapping activities, and missing labels. We propose a fully unsupervised spatiotemporal feature fusion framework using a memory-augmented autoencoder. It enhances activity representations via short temporal windows of multi-sensor IMU data, enabling real-time applications. Our framework extracts hierarchical static features via a Stacked Autoencoder, fusing them within and across sensors. A sequence-to-sequence LSTM Autoencoder then temporally refines these features, incorporating historical motion patterns without labels. We analyze key hyperparameters to identify configurations that maximize feature separability under short-window constraints. Evaluated on DaLiAc and PAMAP2 using realistic inter-class window segmentation, our method achieves 96.6% and 98.4% accuracy, respectively, surpassing supervised baselines and unsupervised approaches. Our method improves feature separability by up to 9% despite shorter temporal windows. While our realistic inter-class segmentation reduces accuracy by ~7%, it was intentionally adopted to better reflect real-world activity transitions and practical relevance.

</details>


### [3] [Zero-Label Driving Scenario Complexity Detection via Joint Embedding Predictive Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28383)
*Santosh Jaiswal*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 用零样本方式，以自监督时序预测误差作为“复杂度分数”，在nuPlan mini的结构化状态数据上，能自动挑出无保护转弯、斑马线交互、行人接近等高风险/高复杂场景，并在异常检测上优于机会基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模未标注驾驶数据中寻找复杂/安全关键场景昂贵且依赖先验（人工标注、监督分类器或规则）。作者探问：能否完全无标签地让模型自身发现“复杂度”。

Method: 训练一个最小化的JEPA（联合嵌入预测架构）作为自监督潜在世界模型，对结构化多智能体状态序列进行时序预测；将预测误差作为零样本复杂度分数。进行四个消融以定位信号来源，并用下游异常检测评估。

Result: 无需任何真值标签，模型对无保护转弯、斑马线交互、行人接近给出显著更高分，对巡航跟车、静止交通给出更低分；异常检测平均准确率（AP）0.512，相比机会基线0.436；消融验证了时序预测误差信号的有效性。

Conclusion: 自监督潜在世界模型的时序预测误差可作为实用的驾驶场景复杂度代理，无需先验标签即可在大规模未标注数据中发现关键场景。

Abstract: Identifying complex and safety-critical driving scenarios in large unlabelled datasets is an important but expensive problem. Existing approaches rely on human annotators, supervised classifiers, or carefully engineered rule sets, all of which require substantial prior knowledge about what constitutes a difficult scenario. We ask whether a model can discover scenario complexity on its own, with no labels at any stage. We train a minimal Joint Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA) on structured agent state data from the nuPlan mini dataset and use the temporal prediction error as a zero-shot complexity score. Without access to any ground-truth labels during training or evaluation setup, the model assigns significantly higher scores to scenarios involving unprotected turns, crosswalk interactions, and pedestrian proximity, and significantly lower scores to lane-following and stationary-traffic scenarios. We validate this finding through four ablation experiments that isolate the source of the signal, and through a downstream anomaly detection evaluation that achieves Average Precision of 0.512 against a 0.436 chance baseline. The results show that temporal prediction error in a self-supervised latent world model is a practical proxy for driving scenario complexity.

</details>


### [4] [Data Provenance for Image Auto-Regressive Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28386)
*Bihe Zhao,Louis Kerner,Michel Meintz,Tameem Bakr,Franziska Boenisch,Adam Dziedzic*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出一种事后（post-hoc）溯源框架，利用图像自回归模型在生成过程中留下的特征模式，无需水印或模型改动，即可鲁棒检测并追溯生成图像至源模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IAR 图像在视觉上常与真实图像难以区分，易被用于虚假信息传播、欺诈与有害内容传播。现有水印方法要求事先嵌入或修改生成流程，无法覆盖已发布或未集成水印的模型与内容，亟需一种无需先验标记且可鲁棒溯源的方案。

Method: 观察与实证发现：IAR 的逐token预测与采样机制在输出中引入可检测的特征模式。基于此，构建一个后验检测框架，在不修改生成流程或输出的情况下，对图像进行特征提取与分类判别，以识别这些IAR特征并据此进行来源模型追踪。

Result: 在多种主流 IAR 上验证，方法能稳定检测并区分由不同 IAR 生成的图像，与真实图像区分度高，展示出良好的鲁棒性与泛化能力，支持有效的模型级溯源。

Conclusion: IAR 生成会留下可利用的固有模式；所提事后框架能在无需水印或流程改动的前提下实现强健溯源，适用于已发布内容与不支持水印的模型，具备在自回归图像生成领域广泛落地的潜力。

Abstract: Image autoregressive models (IARs) have recently demonstrated remarkable capabilities in visual content generation, achieving photorealistic quality and rapid synthesis through the next-token prediction paradigm adapted from large language models. As these models become widely accessible, robust data provenance is required to reliably trace IAR-generated images to the source model that synthesized them. This is critical to prevent the spread of misinformation, detect fraud, and attribute harmful content. We find that although IAR-generated images often appear visually identical to real images, their generation process introduces characteristic patterns in their outputs, which serves as a reliable provenance signal for the generated images. Leveraging this, we present a post-hoc framework that enables the robust detection of such patterns for provenance tracing. Notably, our framework does not require modifications of the generative process or outputs. Thereby, it is applicable in contexts where prior watermarking methods cannot be used, such as for generated content that is already published without additional marks and for models that do not integrate watermarking. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach across a wide range of IARs, highlighting its high potential for robust data provenance tracing in autoregressive image generation.

</details>


### [5] [SoccerNet 2026 Player-Centric Ball Action Spotting: Per-Player Attention with Agreement-Based Ensembling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28389)
*Faisal Altawijri,Ismail Mathkour*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出用于SoccerNet 2026以球员为中心的球权动作定位挑战的两阶段系统：TAAD从转播视频输出逐球员动作logits，DST Transformer将比赛状态与logits转为结构化事件；通过架构改进、注意力设计与集成融合，将Macro-F1从48.6提升到58.94。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有转播视频中精确、以球员为中心的动作定位难，单阶段或缺乏时序/多球员交互建模的方法易误报、召回差；需要结合跟踪、时空上下文与强鲁棒的序列解码，同时在低频类别（如铲球）上维持性能。

Method: 两阶段流水线：1) TAAD：引入时间Transformer进行跨帧上下文建模，并配合若干训练修复；输出逐球员动作logits。2) DST：提出两阶段逐球员注意力，先跨球员后时间的空间优先次序；将比赛状态特征与TAAD logits转录为结构化事件序列。3) 训练四个架构多样的变体，使用加权事件融合与一致性过滤，抑制单模型误报；对稀有“tackle”类别设专门例外以保召回。

Result: 空间优先的注意力顺序带来验证集Macro-F1 +1.87%；最终系统在挑战上将Macro-F1从48.6提升到58.94。

Conclusion: 结合跟踪感知检测、时空解码与多模型加权融合能显著提高以球员为中心的动作定位鲁棒性与准确率；空间优先注意力与针对稀有类的策略有效，整体达成显著的宏平均F1提升。

Abstract: We present our submission to the SoccerNet 2026 Player-Centric Ball Action Spotting challenge, which uses a two-stage pipeline: a Track-Aware Action Detector (TAAD) produces per-player action logits from broadcast video, and a Denoising Sequence Transduction (DST) transformer converts game-state features and TAAD logits into structured event sequences. We improve the TAAD with a temporal transformer that adds cross-frame context, alongside several training fixes. For the DST stage, we introduce a two-stage per-player attention mechanism operating on game-state features, and show that a spatial-first attention ordering (cross-player attention before temporal attention) improves validation Macro-F1 by 1.87%. To exploit architectural diversity, we train four model variants and combine them with a Weighted Event Fusion ensemble that applies agreement filtering to suppress single-model false positives while preserving recall, plus a dedicated exception for the rare tackle class. Our final system improves the challenge Macro-F1 from a baseline of 48.6 to 58.94.

</details>


### [6] [Automated Quality Assessment of Geospatial Vector Data: A GeoAI Approach using Spatial Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28390)
*Hao Li,Chen Chu,Filip Biljecki,Cyrus Shahabi,Wenwen Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Topo4Vec提出一种面向原生矢量数据的自动化GeoAI框架，通过拓扑错误模拟与空间表征学习，实现可扩展的矢量数据质量评估；在三个城市验证，建筑重叠检测达0.99准确率，道路端点错误（overshoot/undershoot）达0.60。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于规则的质量评估在复杂城市形态与大规模数据下表现受限；GeoAI虽兴起，但对原生矢量（线/面）数据的自动质量评估研究不足，需要一种无需大量人工标注、可扩展且鲁棒的方法。

Method: 1) 通过仿真生成带标签的拓扑错误样本（如重叠多边形、道路网络连通性错误overshoot/undershoot），减少人工标注成本；2) 采用先进空间表征学习（SRL）方法，将复杂矢量几何（折线、多边形）编码到潜在空间，使含错与无错样本可分离；3) 在洛杉矶、慕尼黑、新加坡三地进行系统评估。

Result: Topo4Vec在建筑物重叠多边形检测中最高准确率达0.99；在道路网络overshoot/undershoot检测中准确率达0.60；在多城市场景下表现稳健。代码与数据公开。

Conclusion: Topo4Vec证明了通过错误模拟+SRL可在无需大量人工标注的情况下实现可扩展的矢量数据质量监测，为大规模地理空间生态中的一致性与质量监控提供了自动化、可复用的GeoAI路径。

Abstract: Geospatial vector data quality is a foundational research topic in GIS, yet classic rule-based quality assessment algorithms often struggle with diverse urban morphologies and massive data volumes. Recently, Geospatial Artificial Intelligence (GeoAI) shows promising potential for automating geospatial analysis, while its application to native vector data remains largely underexplored. To fill this research gap, we proposed Topo4Vec, an automated GeoAI framework, designed for scalable vector data quality assessment via advanced Spatial Representation Learning (SRL). Specifically, Topo4Vec relax the labor-intensive manual annotation process via topological error simulation, such as overlapping polygons and street network connectivity errors e.g., overshoots and undershoots. Then, it leverages state-of-the-art SRL approaches to encode complex, native vector geometries (e.g., polylines and polygons) into a latent space where topological errors are isolated from valid ones. A systematic performance evaluation across three study areas (Los Angeles, Munich, and Singapore) demonstrates the effectiveness and robustness of Topo4Vec, achieving a peak accuracy of 0.99 for detecting overlapping building footprints and 0.60 for overshoots and undershoots in street networks. Moreover, lessons learned from Topo4Vec shed a promising light into a scalable and autonomous GeoAI approach for large-scale vector data consistency and quality monitoring within the fast-growing geospatial data ecosystems. The code and data used in the paper are made openly available in https://figshare.com/s/612148eeb4bccadbd715.

</details>


### [7] [Few-class Fidelity: Evaluating Explanations of Real-conditions CNN classifiers with Optimized Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28391)
*Wistan Marchadour,Pedro Soto Vega,Franck Vermet,Mathieu Hatt*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种面向少类别、真实应用场景的忠实度（Fidelity）型XAI评估变体，通过生成分布内但引发不确定性的扰动来衡量解释方法的忠实性，并用医学与自然图像实验验证，与人类标注的定位/分割指标对照，揭示领域、数据策划与XAI选择之间的复杂关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有XAI方法众多、评估标准分裂，尤其在真实部署（常为小类数问题）中难以就“解释是否忠实于模型”达成一致；需要一种更贴近实际分布、能客观度量忠实度并与人类感知指标对照的评估框架。

Method: 提出Fidelity度量的变体：在模型训练后，构造“分布内、能激发不确定性”的扰动样本，对比扰动前后模型输出与解释热图（如显著性图）的一致性，以评估解释方法的忠实性；同时与人类中心的定位与分割指标（如bbox/seg）进行对照分析；在医疗与自然图像数据上开展实验。

Result: 新度量在小类别、真实条件下更能区分不同XAI方法的忠实性；与人类定位/分割指标对比显示，二者不总一致，但能互补；实验表明数据领域与策划方式显著影响XAI评估结果与方法优劣。

Conclusion: 评估XAI需兼顾模型内在忠实度与人类可理解性；所提基于分布内不确定性扰动的Fidelity变体为真实场景（低类别）提供更可靠的比较工具，并提醒在新CNN部署前应结合领域、数据策划与XAI方案进行联合验证。

Abstract: The wide use of Convolutional Neural Networks (CNN) in numerous domains and real-world classification applications is justified by their high precision and automation speed, helping users concentrate on higher-expertise tasks. To better understand the models and avoid bias during deployment, eXplainable Artificial Intelligence (XAI) techniques can be used after training. But as the list of XAI solutions expand, comparisons between them diverge, and consensus over their evaluation cannot be reached. This paper proposes a variation of Fidelity-based XAI metrics, with a focus on real-conditions applications, where the number of classes is often low. The approach generates in-distribution, uncertainty-provoking perturbations, to ensure proper measurement of the XAI methods faithfulness. As demonstration of the evaluation framework usefulness, it is compared with human-centric object localization and segmentation metrics. Once applied to both medical and natural imaging applications, it highlights the intricate correlation between domain, data curation, and XAI solution choices in order to validate training of a new CNN model.

</details>


### [8] [RADIANT-PET: Reasoning-Augmented PET/CT Lesion Segmentation with Large Language Models and Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28392)
*Jiasheng Wang,Tanun Jitwatcharakomol,Piyawadee Jongpradubgiat,Simeng Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出RADIANT-PET：以“高召回分割 + LLM逐病灶裁决”为核心，利用文本化的多尺度上下文与强化学习优化的本地LLM，在AutoPET与OSU数据上优于纯图像基线，尤其在引入报告时显著降低生理性假阳性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PET/CT病灶分割易被生理摄取与伪影误导，常规像素级/体素级方法难以在全身复杂背景下可靠地区分真病灶与假阳性；需要一种能结合影像与临床语义、进行病灶级推理的机制，以贴近放射科医生的判读。

Method: 两阶段框架：1) 有意“宽松”的高敏感体素级分割，生成候选摄取区；2) 将每个候选转写为结构化文本（强度、形态、局部/全局解剖位置信息），并由LLM判定真/假病灶与解剖部位；可选地引入放射科报告作为上下文。为强化病灶级推理，采用Group Relative Policy Optimization对本地LLM做强化学习，奖励正确分类与部位一致性。

Result: 在AutoPET与OSU测试集上，较强力图像仅基线均有稳定提升；当提供报告时收益更大；主要改进来自抑制生理性假阳性并使体素级预测更符合临床解读。

Conclusion: 在常规分割之上加入LLM病灶级推理能有效对抗假阳性并对齐临床语义。RADIANT-PET展示了影像-文本协同与RL优化的可行性与优势，代码已开源（见项目仓库）。

Abstract: Accurate lesion segmentation in PET/CT is critical for oncology, yet remains challenging because physiologic tracer uptake and artifacts can mimic malignant signal. We present RADIANT-PET, a reasoning-augmented framework that couples a high-sensitivity voxel-level segmentation model with lesion-level large language model (LLM) adjudication. Candidate uptake regions are generated with a deliberately permissive segmentation stage, then converted into structured textual descriptions that summarize uptake intensity, morphology, and regional and global anatomical context. An LLM classifies each candidate as true lesion vs. false positive, optionally leveraging the radiology report as additional clinical context. To strengthen lesion-level reasoning, we further optimize a local LLM via reinforcement learning using Group Relative Policy Optimization, rewarding correct lesion classification and anatomically concordant site assignment. Across AutoPET and an OSU test cohort, RADIANT-PET consistently outperforms strong image-only baselines, with the largest improvements observed when radiology reports are provided. Overall, these results demonstrate that LLM-based lesion-level reasoning adds a novel reasoning layer beyond conventional segmentation, suppressing physiologic false positives and aligning voxel-level predictions with clinical interpretation. The project repository is available at: https://github.com/jwang-580/RADIANT-PET.

</details>


### [9] [Transition-Aware best-of-N sampling for Longitudinal Chest X-ray Reports](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28393)
*Halil Ibrahim Gulluk,Max Van Puyvelde,Wim Van Criekinge,Olivier Gevaert*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种无需再训练的、面向纵向随访场景的胸片报告生成“最佳N中选优”采样策略，通过显式建模“前次→本次”的转变来挑选更合适的生成报告，显著优于随机选择，尤其在Impression部分提升最大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床读片高度依赖对比前后检查的变化，而现有预训练胸片报告生成器多忽略纵向变化信息。需要一种在不重新训练模型的前提下，利用历史—当前检查差异来改进候选报告选择的机制。

Method: 提出“转变感知的最佳N采样”。步骤：1) 将每份报告切分为句子并嵌入为无序集合向量；2) 通过集合到集合的定向距离将（先前、当前）报告对映射为固定维度的“转变向量”；3) 将候选报告对应的转变向量与缓存的训练集中真实转变向量库做余弦相似度匹配，并以min或kNN方式聚合得分；4) 选取得分最高的候选。实现了四种定向集合距离：均值位移（mean-shift）、新颖残差（novelty residual）、定向Hausdorff锚点、代价加权最优传输（OT）。在多次就诊AP-PA数据上，结合三种提示与三种视觉-语言生成器进行推断评估。

Result: 在所有设置中，“转变感知的最佳N采样”均优于随机候选选择，提升在Impression小节最为显著。

Conclusion: 显式建模纵向“前→今”变化并以无需再训练的选优策略对预训练报告生成模型进行后处理，可稳定提升临床相关的报告质量，尤其在总结变化的Impression部分效果最好。

Abstract: In longitudinal clinical practice, every chest X-ray is read in the context of the patients prior exam, and much of what the radiologist communicates is the change from one visit to the next. To the best of our knowledge, we present the first training-free best-of-N sampling scheme for pre-trained chest X-ray report generators that is explicitly aware of this longitudinal prior to current transition. We call it transition-aware best-of-N sampling, each report is split into sentences and embedded into an unordered set in Rd; each (prior, current) pair is reduced to a fixed-dim directional vector via a set-to-set distance designed to encode the change between the two sets; and candidates are scored by cosine distance from their candidate transition vector to a cached bank of ground-truth training transition vectors, aggregated as min or kNN. We instantiate the framework with four directional set distances (mean-shift, novelty residual, directed-Hausdorff anchor, and cost-weighted optimal transport) and evaluate on a multi-visit AP-PA cohort, running inference under three prompts on three vision-language generators. Transition-aware best-of-N outperforms random selection across the board, with the largest relative gains on the Impression section.

</details>


### [10] [GPU-Accelerated Inverse Structural Anastylosis from Block Collapse Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28394)
*L. A. Muñoz*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Jenga Inverse Predictor (JIP-2)，用GPU加速的深度学习与刚体物理引擎，把“坍塌石块堆”逆推回最可能的原始塔式配置，实现半自动化的建筑遗构复原。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实体遗迹“再拼装”（anastylosis）高度依赖专家经验、手工比对，费时且主观；其组合复杂度类似Jenga游戏的块体去除与稳定性问题，促使作者用可规模化、可复现实验的计算方法降低主观性与人力成本。

Method: 1) 构建完整刚体物理引擎：OBB/SAT碰撞、PGS接触求解，Numba JIT与CuPy CUDA加速；2) 依据Ziglar(2006)解析力阈：Y轴无扭矩F=3μ_smg，X轴有扭矩风险F=4μ_smg，在μ_s∈{0.25,0.40,0.60}下跑450个仿真剧集；3) 训练双流ResNet-18，注入摩擦one-hot，联合预测：可移除块数量、各位置移除概率、质心失衡、Ziglar扭矩风险；4) 生成逐块“逆向重建”的平滑3D视频。

Result: 模型在仿真数据上能从坍塌图像中高准确率地估计原塔配置相关指标与风险，并给出连贯的逐步回溯重建序列，显示出减少人工比对与提升客观性的潜力。

Conclusion: JIP-2将物理建模与深度学习结合，把坍塌结构的复原转化为逆预测问题，可为考古建筑的计算机辅助anastylosis（如尤卡坦Uxmal遗址）提供新工具；论文给出端到端管线与损失设计细节，为今后在真实遗址数据上的扩展与验证奠定基础。

Abstract: The physical anastylosis of collapsed architectural monuments -- the meticulous reassembly of fallen stone elements into their original structural configuration -- represents one of the most intellectually demanding challenges in conservation science. Traditional approaches depend heavily on expert archaeologist judgement and manual block-by-block correspondence, a process that is both labour-intensive and inherently subjective. Inspired by the combinatorial complexity of this problem as manifested in the game of Jenga, we present Jenga Inverse Predictor , a GPU-accelerated deep learning framework that addresses structural anastylosis as an inverse prediction task. Given an image of a collapsed block assembly, JIP-2 reconstructs the most probable prior tower configuration by: (1) implementing a complete rigid-body physics engine with OBB/SAT collision detection and a Projected Gauss-Seidel (PGS) contact solver accelerated with Numba JIT and CuPy CUDA; (2) applying the analytical force thresholds of Ziglar (CMU, 2006) -- F_app = 3*mu_s*m*g (Y-axis, torque-free) and F_app = 4*mu_s*m*g (X-axis, torque risk) -- over three friction levels (mu_s in {0.25, 0.40, 0.60}) across 450 simulated episodes; (3) training a dual-stream ResNet-18 that injects a friction one-hot vector and jointly predicts block removal count, per-position removal probabilities, centre-of-mass imbalance, and Ziglar torque risk; and (4) generating a smooth 3-D video of the block-by-block reverse reconstruction. We discuss implications for computer-assisted anastylosis at the UNESCO Maya site of Uxmal, Yucatan, and provide a detailed technical description of the full pipeline, architecture, and loss formulation.

</details>


### [11] [JASPR: Joint Spatial Representation learning of histology and spatial genomics for improved virtual genomic screening and clinical prognostication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28395)
*Marija Pizurica,Eric Zimmermann,Neil Tenenholtz,James Hall,Olivier Gevaert,Ava P. Amini,Lorin Crawford,Kristen A. Severson*

Method: 提出自监督框架JASPR：以跨模态重建为学习目标，将HE图像块与ST空间点互相预测；在目标中显式建模HE与ST各自的空间邻域信息；使用共享模块学习通用空间属性，辅以模态特定专家提取形态与基因表达的专属特征，联合优化得到共同嵌入。

Conclusion: 跨模态、含空间上下文的自监督学习能有效整合形态与转录信息，获得更强的联合表示，既提高从HE推断分子状态的准确性，也提供临床预后价值。

Abstract: Recent studies have shown that spatial properties of tumors are critical for understanding disease biology and predicting patient outcomes. These spatial properties are increasingly uncovered through complementary modalities: spatial transcriptomics (ST) captures spatially-resolved molecular states, while hematoxylin and eosin-stained whole slide images (HE) reveal tissue morphology. While approaches are emerging to fuse these modalities, effective methods that learn not only joint representations but also incorporate spatial context across modalities are lacking. Here, we present JASPR (Joint Spatial Representation learning), a self-supervised deep learning framework that integrates HE images and ST data through a cross-modal reconstruction objective that incorporates spatial context within HE images and ST profiles. It employs shared modules to capture universal spatial properties across modalities, while modality-specific experts encode features unique to morphological and genomic data. We train and validate JASPR on breast cancer datasets, demonstrating that its learned joint representation substantially improves HE-based prediction of 9,248 genes and provides prognostic value for breast cancer outcomes.

### [12] [RadarTwin: Scene-Specific mmWave Radar Simulation and Learning for Mobile Indoor Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28396)
*Emily Bejerano,Federico Tondolo,Devang Gupta,Aaron Mano Cherian,Taeyoo Kim,Ayaan Qayyum,Xiaofan Yu,Xiaofan Jiang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RadarTwin 是一个在真实采集前、基于目标空间3D重建生成“部署特定”毫米波雷达训练数据的框架；通过材质推断与物理仿真（含多跳反射）合成FMCW雷达信号，并证明这些仿真特征可迁移到现实，在零标签与小样本条件下显著提升识别性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 毫米波雷达数据稀缺、域泛化差：在新物体/环境/轨迹上表现不佳。需要一种在真实部署前即可生成高保真、可迁移的数据来训练模型，减轻真实标注与采集成本，并回答“仿真到现实能转移什么、需要哪些物理因素（如多径）”。

Method: 1) 输入：目标空间的3D重建（手机LiDAR、机器人传感或RGB到3D）。2) 材质理解：用视觉-语言模型推断与雷达相关的表面材料。3) 物理仿真：基于物理的射线追踪器合成多跳传播下的FMCW原始雷达回波。4) 数据集：采集成对的真实-仿真数据，涵盖家庭物体、材质、距离、姿态、平移与移动轨迹，用于分析可迁移性。5) 训练：用纯仿真数据学表示，再用少量真实标签微调/评估。

Result: - 仿真与真实在“可区分物体”的形状与材质特征上一致；必须建模环境多径才能匹配真实测量。- 仅用仿真训练的表示在无真实标签下达到约2.5×随机猜测的识别准确率。- 加入少量真实标注后，在12类识别任务上达95.3%准确率。

Conclusion: RadarTwin可在无真实雷达数据前为特定部署空间预训练雷达感知模型；关键在于材质推断与多径物理仿真。所学表示具备跨域可迁移性，少量真实数据即可达到接近全面监督的性能。

Abstract: Millimeter-wave (mmWave) radar perception is limited by data scarcity: models trained on existing radar datasets fail to generalize to new objects, environments, and sensing trajectories. We present RadarTwin, a framework for generating deployment-specific radar training data before real data collection. Given a 3D reconstruction of a target space (phone LiDAR, robot-mounted sensing, or RGB-to-3D), RadarTwin uses a vision-language model to infer radar-relevant surface materials and a physics-based ray tracer to synthesize raw frequency-modulated continuous-wave (FMCW) radar measurements with multi-bounce propagation. To study what transfers from simulation to reality, we collect a paired real-simulated dataset spanning household objects, material classes, distances, rotations, translations, and mobile sensing trajectories. We show that simulated and real radar share the same object-discriminative shape and material features, and that modeling the environment's multipath is essential to matching real measurements. A representation trained on simulation alone recognizes real objects at 2.5 times chance with no real radar labels, and a few labeled examples raise this to 95.3% on a 12-way recognition task. RadarTwin enables training radar perception for a new space before any real radar data is collected there.

### [13] [CLOSER-VLN: Closed-Loop Self-Verified Retrieval-Augmented Reasoning for Aerial Vision-Language Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28397)
*Shaoxuan Li,Xiangyu Dong,Xiaoguang Ma,Junfeng Chen,Haoran Zhao,Yaoming Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CLOSER：一种闭环、自验证、检索增强的推理框架，在执行动作前完成“推理-校验-检索-纠正”的闭环以减少误差累积；在CityNav无人机导航上显著提升SR与SPL（SR 32.01%、SPL 21.28%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有依赖大模型的VLN多为开环：基于指令与观测生成动作后直接执行，缺少执行前的可靠性核验与纠错，导致尤其在空中导航中小错易迅速累积致轨迹偏离和目标丢失。需要一种在不训练特定策略的前提下，能自我核验并有针对性利用外部经验的机制。

Method: 提出CLOSER（Closed-loop Self-verified Retrieval-augmented Reasoning）：在执行前循环进行四步：1) 分层推理器基于可用信息生成候选动作；2) 多维度动作验证器评估动作可靠性；3) 若验证失败，触发多模态检索，从记忆库检索与当前情境最相关的示例；4) 根据检索与验证结果进行动作纠正；之后才执行。实例化为CLOSER-VLN用于空中VLN任务。

Result: 在CityNav基准的test-unseen上，CLOSER-VLN达到SR 32.01%、SPL 21.28%，优于开环方法，验证闭环推理与自验证、检索增强机制的有效性。

Conclusion: 闭环、自验证、按需检索并纠正的框架能有效缓解空中VLN中误差累积问题，在无需训练专用导航策略的前提下提升泛化与稳健性。

Abstract: Vision-language navigation (VLN) has recently advanced with large language and multimodal models, enabling agents to follow natural-language instructions in unseen environments without training a task-specific navigation policy. However, most existing VLN methods relying on large models still adopt an open-loop decision-execution approach, where candidate actions are generated from instructions and observations but are rarely verified or corrected before execution. This causes critical issues in aerial VLN, where minor errors in intermediate actions may quickly accumulate into large trajectory deviations and lead to target loss. To address this issue, we propose Closed-loop Self-verified Retrieval-augmented Reasoning (CLOSER), a training-policy-free method that sequentially performs action reasoning, reliability verification, targeted retrieval, and action correction in a closed-loop manner before executing concrete actions. We instantiate the CLOSER in aerial VLN tasks and develop a CLOSER-VLN framework, which is composed of three components: a hierarchical reasoner for generating candidate actions based on available information, a multidimensional action verifier for assessing the reliability of actions generated by the reasoner, and a verification-triggered multimodal retriever for retrieving targeted exemplars from a memory bank only when verification fails. We conduct experimental evaluations on the CityNav benchmark, where CLOSER-VLN achieves 32.01% SR and 21.28% SPL on the test-unseen split, confirming the effectiveness of closed-loop reasoning.

</details>


### [14] [Semantic-Aware Generative Image Transmission for Resource-Constrained Visual IoT Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28398)
*Chenyang Zhang,Changwang Liu,Jinqi Zhu,Jiayi Chang,Yuxuan Wang,Shuqing He,Jia Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种面向资源受限视觉物联网的“语义感知+生成式”图像传输框架：发端只发送少量重要VQ令牌与掩码，云端用MaskGIT按Halton调度补全；在极低码率下兼顾感知质量与下游任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统图像通信多传全局表征或压缩整图，难以让接收端生成式复原发挥作用；窄带无线链路下，视觉IoT需在极低比特率保证任务相关区域（目标/实例）质量，同时适配多种信道（AWGN/Rayleigh）并与下游检测/分析协同。

Method: 1) 用VQ编码器将图像离散化为令牌栅格；2) 在端侧依据两类信号为每个令牌打分：可恢复性（由预测熵与局部结构复杂度估计）与语义重要性（实例分割+类别感知评分）；3) 融合得分并经空间发散采样器在码率预算下选取要传输的令牌；4) 发送保留令牌的量化索引与二值掩码；5) 边/云端用MaskGIT并结合Halton序列调度对被遮蔽令牌进行生成式补全与重建；

Result: - 在Kodak与VisDrone、AWGN/Rayleigh信道上，实现灵活码率-质量折衷；- 于0.074 bpp下，仅用DeepJSCC/WITT在0.167 bpp时比特数的44.6%，达成29.9 dB PSNR；- 在Kodak上的伪GT下游检测实验表明：在30%与50%掩蔽率下，语义感知掩蔽较随机掩蔽更好地保留任务相关目标。

Conclusion: 语义感知选择+生成式补全能在窄带视觉IoT中显著降低上行比特而维持感知质量与任务相关性；方法对多种场景与信道鲁棒，并提供可调的带宽-质量权衡。

Abstract: Resource-constrained visual Internet of Things (IoT) systems, such as edge cameras, unmanned sensing platforms, industrial inspection nodes, and remote monitoring sensors, often need to transmit task-relevant visual evidence over low-rate wireless links to an edge/cloud service. Existing image communication methods usually compress or transmit complete global representations, leaving limited room to exploit receiver-side generative restoration. This paper proposes a semantic-aware generative image transmission framework for edge-assisted visual IoT. The image captured by an IoT visual sensor is encoded into a discrete token grid by a VQ encoder. At the IoT transmitter or nearby gateway, token recoverability, estimated from prediction entropy and local structure complexity, is fused with semantic importance obtained from instance segmentation and category-aware scoring. A spatial dispersal sampler then selects the tokens to be transmitted under a bitrate budget. The transmitter sends only the quantization indices of kept tokens and a binary mask map, while the edge/cloud receiver recovers masked tokens through MaskGIT with Halton sequence scheduling. Experiments on Kodak and VisDrone scenes under AWGN and Rayleigh channels show that the proposed method provides a flexible bitrate-quality tradeoff for narrowband visual IoT links. At 0.074 bpp, it uses 44.6% of the transmitted bits of the 0.167-bpp DeepJSCC/WITT reference while achieving 29.9 dB PSNR. A pseudo-GT downstream detection study on Kodak further shows that semantic-aware masking preserves task-relevant objects better than random masking at both 30% and 50% mask ratios.

### [15] [Meta-learning as a principle for human-like visual representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28399)
*Can Demircan,Marcel Binz,Alireza Modirshanechi,Eric Schulz*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 作者提出：人类视觉表征之所以更贴近开放式任务需求，是因为受到“元学习（学会如何学习）”的压力而形成。用跨数千个语义任务进行序列元学习得到的表示，在预测人类相似度判断、语义规则学习与高级视觉皮层响应上，均优于仅预训练的基础编码器。行为收益依赖任务分布的可分解与高层语义性；而与大脑一致性的提升主要由元学习压力驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预训练视觉网络虽能较好拟合人类视觉表征，但仍存在明显差距；原因之一或在于这些网络只优化单一固定目标，而人类须应对开放式、快速迁移的新任务。作者欲检验：若让模型在多样高层语义任务上进行“学会如何学”，其得到的表示能否更接近人类。

Method: 训练一个序列模型，在无任何人类数据监督下，跨数千个将图像映射到高层概念的语义任务进行元学习（少样本、快速适应）。与其对应的仅预训练的基础编码器进行比较。评估维度包括：预测人类相似性判断、语义规则学习行为，以及与高级视觉皮层（神经影像/神经表征相似性）的对齐。并分析任务分布属性（是否高层/可解缠）与“学习-如何-学习”压力对结果的影响。

Result: 与基础编码器相比，元学习后的表示在三方面显著更贴近人类：（1）更好预测人类相似度判断；（2）更好解释人类的语义规则学习与类推行为；（3）与高层视觉皮层活动的对齐更强。消融分析显示：行为层面的增益依赖于任务分布的可解缠与高层语义性；而脑对齐的改进主要由元学习压力本身驱动。

Conclusion: 人类视觉表征的灵活性可能源于在环境中持续需要“随时学习新语义关系”的功能性需求。将元学习压力注入视觉表征训练，可缩小模型与人类在行为与神经层面的差距，提示未来应关注多任务、可快速适应的训练范式，而非单一固定目标的预训练。

Abstract: The structure of human visual representations underpins our capacity for adaptive behaviour. While pretrained neural networks model human visual representations with unprecedented success, a large discrepancy remains. We propose one reason: these networks optimise a single fixed objective, whereas human representations must support open-ended tasks. We hypothesise this flexibility arises from meta-learning (learning to learn), a pressure shaping representations to acquire new tasks from few observations. To test this, we train a sequence model, without any supervision from human data, across thousands of semantically rich tasks mapping images to high-level concepts. Compared to their pretrained base encoders, meta-learned representations better predict human similarity judgements, semantic rule learning, and high-level visual cortex. Behavioural gains depend on disentangled, high-level task distributions, while brain alignment is driven primarily by the learning-to-learn pressure. Our results suggest the flexibility of human visual representations reflects the functional demand to learn new semantic relationships on the fly.

### [16] [Vision-driven Preference Synthesis for Mitigating Hallucinations in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28401)
*Yunhun Nam,Jongheon Jeong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ViPSy提出一种视觉驱动的偏好构造框架，通过从语义相近的图像变体中抽取复发的对象级视觉线索，并用该线索引导模型自身生成候选，从而在不偏离原有策略分布的前提下显著降低幻觉并提升视觉对齐与下游视觉能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM对图像的不实编造（幻觉）仍突出。偏好对齐可缓解，但：1）基于干预的方法会使数据分布偏离策略分布；2）基于采样的方法在构造偏好时对视觉证据利用不足、受语言先验影响大。因此需要一种既贴近模型策略分布、又强依赖真实视觉信息的偏好数据构造方法。

Method: ViPSy包含两阶段：1）视觉线索提取：对一组语义对齐的图像变体，挖掘反复出现的对象级内容，形成可显式注入的视觉cue，使后续偏好构造依托图像证据而非语言先验。2）策略受控生成：在该视觉cue条件下，用模型自身进行rollout生成候选响应，使候选既被视觉内容约束，又与原策略分布保持接近；据此合成偏好对。用这些偏好对进行对齐训练。

Result: 将以ViPSy构造的偏好对用于对齐训练后，新模型在幻觉缓解基准上达SOTA：AMBER与Object HalBench幻觉率分别较先前SOTA下降35.7%与24.5%。同时在通用视觉对齐基准（MMStar、MMVP、CV-Bench）取得提升，并在语义分割与ImageNet线性探测上也有增益。

Conclusion: 以视觉线索驱动且与策略分布一致的偏好构造能有效减少VLM幻觉并广泛增强视觉能力。ViPSy为偏好对齐提供了一条兼顾视觉扎根与分布一致性的通用范式。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have shown strong performance in visual understanding, yet they still suffer from hallucinations, generating content that is not grounded in the image. Preference alignment is a promising approach to improve visual faithfulness, but its success depends heavily on how preference pairs are constructed. Existing methods exhibit two key limitations; (a) intervention-based methods often introduce significant deviation from the policy distribution, and (b) sampling-based methods often underuse visual information during the construction. In this paper, we propose ViPSy (Vision-driven Preference Synthesis), a framework for constructing preference data that are both policy-aligned and visually grounded. Our framework consists of two stages; in the first stage, ViPSy derives a visual cue from recurring object-level content across semantically aligned image variants, so preference construction can rely on visual information rather than language priors. In the second stage, ViPSy conditions the policy's own rollouts on this cue, allowing candidates to be guided by visually grounded content while staying close to the policy's response distribution. The resulting candidates remain close to the policy's response distribution while better leveraging visual information from the image. Experiments show that the resulting VLM, preference-aligned with ViPSy-constructed preference pairs, achieves a new state-of-the-art in hallucination mitigation. Compared with the previous state-of-the-art method, it reduces hallucination rates on AMBER and Object HalBench by 35.7% and 24.5%, respectively. The resulting model further improves on general visual grounding benchmarks, e.g., MMStar, MMVP, and CV-Bench, while also yielding gains in semantic segmentation and ImageNet linear probing, underscoring the effectiveness of our framework in enhancing the model's visual capabilities.

</details>


### [17] [DCSNet: Multiscale Feature Aggregation for Small Medical Object Segmentation with Detection-guided Hierarchical Cropping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28402)
*Shanfeng Zhang,Bo Gou,Yue Cao,Lei Zhang,Zhang Yi,Tao He*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DCSNet，通过“检测引导裁剪+多尺度特征聚合”实现从全局密集分割到局部精修，显著提升小目标与边界分割表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小目标在医学影像中稀疏且边界复杂，导致类别不平衡与边界退化；传统全局分割网络易漏检小目标、边缘模糊，需要一种既能抑制背景干扰又能细化边界的方案。

Method: 端到端DCSNet包含两核心模块：1) 检测引导层级裁剪(DGHC)：利用候选框/区域提议在多层级动态裁剪，提取以目标为中心的特征，过滤大面积背景，缓解类不平衡；2) 多尺度特征聚合(MSFA)：在裁剪后的纯净区域内，结合Transformer编码器与像素自适应融合策略，动态聚合多尺度特征，兼顾全局语义与细粒度细节，实现锋利边界。整体流程为先检后分，局部精修。

Result: 在三个多样化医学数据集上显著优于现有SOTA，尤其在边界精度上有大幅提升，表现稳健，适用于微小病灶分割。

Conclusion: 将全局密集预测转化为检测引导的局部分割，有效缓解类不平衡并强化边界描绘；DCSNet为临床微小病灶分割提供了鲁棒、高精度的解决方案。

Abstract: Small object segmentation in medical imaging is primarily hindered by class imbalance and inherent boundary complexity. Consequently, conventional global networks frequently fail to detect sparse targets or suffer from severe edge degradation. To overcome these limitations, we propose the Detection-guided Cropping Segmentation Network (DCSNet), an end-to-end framework that transforms global dense prediction into a localized refinement process. This framework integrates two core components, namely Detection-guided Hierarchical Cropping (DGHC) and Multiscale Feature Aggregation (MSFA). The DGHC module leverages region proposals to dynamically extract object-centric features, effdataectively filtering out massive background interference to mitigate class imbalance. Subsequently, the MSFA module operates strictly within these purified regions, synergizing a Transformer encoder with a pixel-adaptive fusion strategy. This mechanism dynamically aggregates multiscale features to capture both semantic context and fine-grained details for sharp boundary delineation. Extensive experiments across three diverse medical datasets demonstrate that DCSNet significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods, yielding substantial improvements in boundary precision and offering a highly robust solution for clinical micro-lesion segmentation.

### [18] [Enhancing Layer Interaction Using Key-Correlated Layer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28405)
*Jianlong Xiong,ChuanBo Xie,Le Yu,Quansong He,Tao He*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种Key-Correlated Layer Attention (KCLA)，以线性复杂度替代层注意力的二次复杂度，同时保持动态更新与长程跨层连接，在多任务上验证有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统层注意力需每层查询所有先前层，带来随深度呈二次增长的计算成本。已有的RLA与线性注意力虽降复杂度，但更新静态、难以建模长程跨层依赖，影响表达力与性能。

Method: 观察到层注意力中的Key表示在不同层间具有高余弦相似性，基于此提出KCLA：在保持由层注意力定义直接推导的动态信息更新的同时，通过对Key的相关性建模实现线性时间复杂度；空间复杂度固定且与网络深度无关；仍保留长程跨层连接能力。

Result: 在图像识别、目标检测、医学图像分割等多种任务上取得良好表现，表明在保证效率的同时维持或提升精度。

Conclusion: KCLA利用Key间高相似性的结构性特征，将层注意力的计算降为线性且保持动态与长程依赖，空间开销固定，具有广泛适用性与实际价值。

Abstract: Recent advances in network architecture design have introduced layer attention to enhance inter-layer interactions. In such frameworks, each layer queries all preceding layers to establish cross-layer connections. However, layer attention results in quadratic computational complexity with respect to network depth. To mitigate this issue, prior works have proposed Recurrent Layer Attention (RLA) and linear attention mechanisms, which suffer from static information updates and limited long-range cross-layer dependency modeling. To overcome these limitations, we propose Key-Correlated Layer Attention (KCLA), inspired by our observation that Key representations in layer attention exhibit high cosine similarity. KCLA achieves linear computational complexity while preserving dynamic information updates, directly derived from the foundational definition of layer attention. Furthermore, KCLA maintains long-range cross-layer connections and features a fixed spatial complexity, independent of network depth. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that KCLA delivers good performance across diverse tasks, including image recognition, object detection, and medical image segmentation. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/bgx666/KCLA.

</details>

Result: 在多组遥感数据集上，RSGPNet在定量与定性指标上均优于现有SOTA，尤其在类边界与复杂场景中表现更稳健，并展现良好可解释性。

Abstract: Open-vocabulary semantic segmentation (OVSS) enables text-guided segmentation of unseen objects, breaking fixed-class limitations to achieve open-world understanding. However, existing OVSS methods primarily focus on modifying the CLIP attention mechanism, which still suffers from unstable local segmentation for remote sensing (RS) domain. To address these limitations, we propose RSGPNet, a training-free geometric prompting framework for RS OVSS that refines segmentation by leveraging object geometric areas and consistency constraints. Specifically, RSGPNet comprises three core modules: a Text-guided Coarse Mask module (TCM), a Geometric Re-prompting Module (GRP), and a Coarse-to-fine Consistency Verification Mechanism (CVM). TCM utilizes text prompts and the input image to construct initial coarse segmentation masks. GRP then converts these coarse masks into geometric box prompts, feeding them back into the segmentation model to generate refined masks. Finally, CVM employs consistency computation to prevent prompting from reinforcing erroneous regions. They allow the model to improve segmentation accuracy in complex areas, such as category boundaries. Extensive experiments on RS datasets demonstrate that RSGPNet significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods across both quantitative and qualitative metrics while exhibiting excellent interpretability. The code is released at \href{https://github.com/wangshanwen001/RSGPNet}{https://github.com/wangshanwen001/RSGPNet}.

### [20] [AEGIS: A Semantic GAN and Evidential Learning Frameworkfor Robust Adversarial Detection in Vision Sensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28416)
*Maher Boughdiri,Mounira Msahli,Albert Bifet*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AEGIS框架：先用SemantiGAN做多类语义一致性判别过滤对抗样本，再对通过者进行随机增强，计算五个不稳定性特征，输入EDL分类器以输出类别与不确定性，实现对多类攻击的高效检测与鲁棒分类，在Tiny-ImageNet上显著优于Softmax检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DNN在视觉传感网络中虽性能优异，但易受对抗扰动与不可感知噪声影响，造成误判；现有基于Softmax的检测在鲁棒性、解释性与不确定性校准上不足，需要一个既能早期过滤语义异常、又能量化预测不稳定性并提供校准不确定性的统一框架。

Method: 1) 语义判别：引入SemantiGAN作为多类语义判别器，先过滤视觉语义不一致的输入；2) 测试时随机增强：对通过的样本进行随机数据增强；3) 特征提取：从增强集计算五维不稳定性特征——FlipScore、预测不一致度、层间余弦相似度（早期/中层）、熵；4) 证据深度学习（EDL）：将五维特征输入EDL，以Dirichlet建模证据，输出类别与校准不确定性。

Result: 在Tiny-ImageNet上，覆盖clean、FGSM、PGD、补丁型、功能型、几何型共六类场景/攻击下，AEGIS取得AUROC 92.1%、AUPRC 90.2%、准确率90.7%，检测/鲁棒性/可解释性/不确定性校准均优于传统Softmax检测方法。

Conclusion: AEGIS通过“语义过滤+不稳定性度量+证据式不确定性”的级联设计，有效检测并缓解多类对抗攻击，提供更可靠、可解释且校准良好的图像分类；可作为视觉传感流水线的稳健前端与后端联合防护方案。

Abstract: Deep neural networks (DNNs) have shown outstanding performance in visual recognition tasks within vision sensor networks; however, they are still vulnerable to adversarial manipulations and imperceptible perturbations that can lead to erroneous predictions. To address that, this paper presents AEGIS, a semantic aware and uncertainty guided adversarial detection framework designed for robust image classification in vision sensors pipelines. At its core, a SemantiGAN module functions as a multi class semantic discriminator, identifying and filtering visually inconsistent adversarial inputs before they propagate further in the pipeline. For inputs that pass this stage, a stochastic augmentation process generates test time variations, from which handcrafted instability metrics FlipScore, Prediction Inconsistency, Layerwise Cosine Similarity (early and mid layers), and Entropy are computed. These features are aggregated into a compact five dimensional vector and processed by an Evidential Deep Learning (EDL) classifier, which models output evidence using a Dirichlet distribution to yield both class predictions and calibrated uncertainty estimates. Evaluations on the Tiny ImageNet dataset across six categories clean, FGSM, PGD, patch based, functional, and geometric attacks demonstrate the effectiveness of AEGIS. The proposed framework achieves an AUROC of 92.1\%, an AUPRC of 90.2\%, and an accuracy of 90.7\%, outperforming conventional softmax-based detectors in terms of detection performance, robustness, interpretability, and uncertainty calibration.

### [21] [DiffRGD: An Inference-Time Diffusion Guidance Through Riemannian Gradient Descent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28417)
*Jia-Wei Liao,Li-Xuan Peng,Mei-Heng Yueh,Min Sun,Cheng-Fu Chou,Jun-Cheng Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DiffRGD：在不微调的前提下，通过黎曼梯度下降在高斯诱导的球面约束上进行推理时引导，显式保持扩散潜变量的高斯结构，从而提升条件/修复类任务的生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理时引导常凭可微目标直接修改潜变量，但会引入分布漂移，破坏原始高斯先验，导致画质/保真度下降；需要一种既能有效控制生成、又不破坏潜在分布结构的方法。

Method: 将每个扩散采样步视为在由潜在高斯分布诱导的球面流形上的约束优化问题；在该流形上用Riemannian Gradient Descent执行引导更新，确保更新后仍处于高斯等范约束；作为即插即用模块，可嵌入任意预训练扩散模型，无需再训练。

Result: 在多种图像修复与条件生成基准上优于以往推理时引导方法，提升了图像质量与任务指标，同时保持采样分布与高斯先验一致性。

Conclusion: 分布感知的球面流形约束与RGD优化能在推理时实现有效可控且不损害先验结构的引导；DiffRGD提供通用、无需微调的方案，兼容主流扩散模型，并带来更佳生成表现。

Abstract: Recently, diffusion models have been widely adopted in generative modeling and have served as foundational models for many image generation tasks. To control the generation without costly re-training or fine-tuning, many works seek inference-time guidance methods to steer the latent via a differentiable objective at inference time. However, these methods cannot effectively preserve the original Gaussian distribution because they introduce distributional drift, thereby degrading the sample quality. To address this gap, we propose DiffRGD, a distribution-aware guidance framework that explicitly preserves the latent Gaussian structure. DiffRGD formulates each sampling step as a constrained optimization problem on a spherical manifold induced by the latent Gaussian distribution, and solves it efficiently via Riemannian Gradient Descent (RGD). DiffRGD is a plug-and-play method that can be seamlessly integrated into any pre-trained diffusion model. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DiffRGD outperforms previous methods in most image restoration and conditional generation tasks. Our codebase is available at https://github.com/jwliao1209/DiffRGD.

</details>


### [22] [MedDiffuseMix: Preserving Diagnostic Evidence with Saliency-Aware Diffusion Medical Image Data Augmentatio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28419)
*Teerath Kumar,Raja Vavekanand,Muhammad Turab*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MedDiffuseMix：一种由显著性引导的扩散式混合增强方法，在低显著区域进行受控混合与扩散，保持诊断关键结构，提升多医学影像数据集上的分类性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学影像分类常受限于样本稀缺、类别不平衡与跨域差异；传统增强可能破坏关键病灶结构，而无约束生成式增强易引入标签不一致内容，需要一种既能扩充多样性又能保护诊断证据的受控增强策略。

Method: 利用已训练分类器的显著图划分高显著（诊断关键）与低显著（背景/非关键）区域；主要在低显著区域进行扩散引导的样本混合，并采用自适应混合比例、高斯边界平滑，以及显著性保持约束；对使关注偏离临床证据的样本进行拒绝或衰减。

Abstract: Limited data availability, class imbalance, and domain variability remain major barriers to reliable medical image classification. Conventional augmentation can improve training diversity but may distort diagnostically informative structures, whereas unconstrained generative augmentation may introduce label-inconsistent content. This paper proposes MedDiffuseMix, a saliency-guided diffusion mixing framework for controlled medical image augmentation. The method uses classifier-derived saliency maps to separate high-saliency diagnostic regions from low-saliency background areas and applies diffusion-guided mixing mainly to regions with lower diagnostic importance. Adaptive mixing, Gaussian boundary blending, and a saliency-preservation constraint reduce semantic distortion and reject or attenuate samples that shift model attention away from clinically relevant evidence. The framework is evaluated on four public benchmarks: the Radiological Society of North America pneumonia chest radiography dataset, Musculoskeletal Radiographs, PatchCamelyon, and the Breast Cancer Histopathological Image Classification dataset. Experiments with convolutional and transformer-based classifiers show that MedDiffuseMix improves accuracy, F1-score, and area under the receiver operating characteristic curve compared with standard augmentation, Mixup, GenMix, SaliencyMix, and diffusion-based augmentation baselines. Ablation studies confirm the importance of saliency guidance, adaptive region mixing, and smooth boundary blending. Visual attribution analysis further indicates that MedDiffuseMix better preserves diagnostically salient regions. These results suggest that saliency-guided diffusion mixing is an effective augmentation strategy for limited-data medical image classification.

### [23] [JuZhou 1.0 Technical Report: The First Edge-Native Text-to-Image Foundation Model Trained Entirely on China-Developed AI Accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28421)
*Ce Chen,Congrui Wang,Yonglin Li,Zhenchen Wan,Mingyang Geng,Junhao Xiao,Zhengpeng Xing,Yaqing Hu,Yao Wu,Zhaoyang Qu,Long Lan,Xinwang Liu,Yingqi Peng,Shijia Li,Zufeng Zhang,Chen Ma,Jingjing Zhou,Xingyu Wang,Qilin Lu,Bin Jiang,Qilin Sun,Shanzhi Gu,Yaoguang Jin,Tongliang Liu,Kede Ma,Yifan Peng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: JuZhou 1.0 是一款超轻量级、可完全离线在端侧运行的中英偏中文原生 T2I 扩散模型，通过小型U-Net+蒸馏解码器、Rectified Flow+DMD2 四步采样、中文语义对齐数据以及国产算力训练，实现接近/优于主流大模型的生成质量与手机端秒级推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: T2I 扩散模型在云端推理成本高、延迟大且有隐私风险，不利于在边缘设备部署；缺乏面向中文原生文本的对齐与端侧可行的高效训练/蒸馏方案。

Method: - 架构：约3.87亿参数的去噪U‑Net（0.385B）+蒸馏解码器（1.90M）。
- 训练与推理：采用 Rectified Flow 训练结合 DMD2 蒸馏，将推理步数降至4步；提供28步基模以衡量上限。
- 数据与对齐：用900万高质量中图文对做中文语义对齐，推理时直接中文提示词，无需翻译。
- 基础设施：在国产 Sugon K100 加速器上完成训练与蒸馏，无依赖 NVIDIA。

Result: 28步基模在 GenEval 得分0.69，优于 SDXL(0.55)、SD3‑Medium(0.62)、IF‑XL(0.61)。在 Snapdragon 8 Elite Gen 5 手机上，4步U‑Net去噪约1.6秒；Android 全流程（含端侧提示优化）约4.5秒；iOS 验证核心生成分支可运行。

Conclusion: JuZhou 1.0 以小模型+高效蒸馏/采样在移动端实现高质量、低延迟、离线的中文原生图生文生成；同时展示了国产算力可完成端到端训练的可行性，为端侧部署与中文生态提供了可复用参考。

Abstract: Text-to-image (T2I) diffusion models typically require substantial computational resources and cloud infrastructure, posing significant challenges for edge deployment in terms of latency, cost, and user privacy. We present JuZhou 1.0, an ultra-lightweight T2I foundation model designed for fully offline, on-device execution. JuZhou 1.0 achieves its efficiency through four key designs: (1) a compact image-generation backbone consisting of a 0.385B-parameter denoising U-Net and a 1.90M-parameter distilled decoder, totaling approximately 0.387B parameters; (2) Rectified Flow training combined with DMD2 distillation, reducing inference to 4 sampling steps; (3) Chinese semantic alignment trained on 9M curated image-text pairs, enabling direct Chinese prompting without external translation at inference time; and (4) a training and distillation pipeline completed on domestically developed Sugon K100 AI accelerators without relying on NVIDIA GPUs for training or distillation. Despite its compact scale, the 28-step base model of JuZhou 1.0 achieves an overall GenEval score of 0.69, outperforming published baselines including SDXL (2.6B, 0.55), SD3-Medium (2B, 0.62), and IF-XL (4.3B, 0.61). We further validate the full poetry-to-image pipeline on Android and the core CLIP-U-Net-VAE generation branch on iOS. On a smartphone powered by the Snapdragon 8 Elite Gen 5 Mobile Platform, the 4-step U-Net denoising branch runs in approximately 1.6 seconds, while the full Android poetry-to-image pipeline takes 4.5 seconds with on-device prompt refinement on Xiaomi 17 Pro Max. These results position JuZhou 1.0 as a practical approach to mobile text-to-image generation and provide a concrete reference for Chinese-native generation, domestic-compute training, and fully offline on-device deployment after one-time installation.

</details>


### [24] [CLEAR-MoE: Shared-Basis Expert Extraction from Frozen Vision Transformers via Calibration-Driven Layer Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28516)
*Md Irtiza Hossain,Humaira Ayesha,Junaid Ahmed Sifat*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CLEAR-MoE 是一个无需更新主干权重、将冻结的ViT转为稀疏MoE的四阶段后训练流程：挑层—分解—训练路由—高效调度；其核心是共享SVD低秩基，几乎不损失精度，但当前在消费级GPU上存在路由与scatter-gather的内存瓶颈与时延开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不改动已训练ViT主干的前提下，获得MoE的稀疏计算与潜在推理效率，同时尽量保持原精度，并研究哪些组件（路由、专家数、秩等）对精度影响关键。

Method: 四步：1) 依据稀疏性、可聚类性与输出敏感度为FFN层打分选层；2) 将选中层按k-means聚类，将FFN分解为共享低秩SVD基+每簇残差专家；3) 用聚类标签监督训练轻量路由器（也尝试随机/不同结构路由）；4) 通过可插拔CUDA后端进行token分发与聚合；并在多骨干上做消融与基准。

Result: 在Imagenette+DeiT-S上，保持99.9%原精度（86.70±0.02% vs 86.73%）；不同路由策略与结构精度几乎一致（差≤0.06pp）；对SVD秩、专家数(2-8)、校准集大小(50-500)、随机种子均稳定；在5个ViT骨干上与致密模型精度差≤0.10pp。速度方面，在GTX 960上由于路由与scatter-gather开销，FFN变慢1.3-1.7倍。

Conclusion: 共享SVD基是保精度的主因，路由细节影响很小。当前主要瓶颈在内存受限的分发与聚合，需融合调度内核以降低开销。方法泛化到多种ViT且几乎不降精度，但实际加速需进一步工程优化。

Abstract: We present CLEAR-MoE, a four-phase post-training pipeline that converts a frozen pretrained Vision Transformer (ViT) into a sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) model without updating backbone weights. The pipeline (i) scores feed-forward network (FFN) layers by sparsity, clusterability, and output sensitivity; (ii) decomposes selected layers into a shared low-rank SVD basis and per-cluster residual experts using k-means clustering; (iii) trains lightweight routers supervised by cluster labels; and (iv) dispatches tokens through pluggable CUDA backends. On Imagenette with DeiT-Small, CLEAR-MoE retains 99.9% of the dense model's accuracy (86.70 +/- 0.02% versus 86.73%). Extensive ablation studies reveal a consistent empirical finding: the shared SVD basis is the primary factor responsible for preserving accuracy. Random routing, learned routing, and three different router architectures produce nearly identical performance, with accuracy varying by at most 0.06 percentage points (86.62%-86.68%). Accuracy also remains stable across different SVD ranks, expert counts (2-8), calibration set sizes (50-500), and random seeds. This behavior generalizes across five ViT backbones (DeiT-Tiny, DeiT-Small, DeiT-Base, ViT-Small, and ViT-Base), covering models from 5.7M to 86.6M parameters, with accuracy differences <= 0.10 percentage points from their dense counterparts. On a GTX 960 GPU, routing and scatter-gather overhead make the CLEAR-MoE FFN 1.3-1.7x slower than the dense implementation. A dispatch microbenchmark further shows that routing is an order of magnitude more memory-bound than expert matrix multiplications, identifying fused dispatch kernels as a promising direction for future optimization.

</details>


### [25] [Detecting Clinical Hallucinations in LVLMs via Counterfactual Visual Grounding Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28520)
*Xiao Song,Haonan Qin,Zhaoxu Zhang,Jiong Zhang,Yuqi Fang,Caifeng Shan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种无需访问或修改LVLM内部的可视证据可追溯幻觉检测框架，通过实体抽取与医学领域适配的Qwen-VL定位验证，并结合反事实实体扰动，计算实体级不确定性以进行二分类检测，跨多模态/多模型显著优于现有方法，且可解释性与可迁移性强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LVLM在临床图像理解中常产生幻觉（报告中出现图像未支持的结论），影响安全与可信度。现有方法往往依赖模型内部特征或缺乏可解释定位与跨模型适用性。需要一种通用、可解释、对不同LVLM可迁移的外部审计方法。

Method: 1) 从LVLM文本响应中抽取可视可核验的医学实体；2) 使用医学领域适配的Qwen-VL作为证据定位验证器，对每个实体在输入图像上进行grounding并输出置信度；3) 设计反事实实体扰动，生成与原实体对立或替代的描述，进行对照grounding；4) 依据正向置信度、反事实置信度及其定位重叠，估计实体级视觉证据不确定性；5) 以该不确定性为依据进行二元幻觉判定并汇总为响应级结论；附带可视化定位证据。

Result: 在多种医学影像模态（如X光、CT等）与多种LVLM骨干上评测，相比近期基线，方法在幻觉检测指标上持续提升，并展现出对不同模型的强迁移性；同时提供可解释的定位可视化。

Conclusion: 所提框架可在黑箱设置下有效审计LVLM临床图像描述中的幻觉，通过反事实增强与不确定性建模实现稳健检测，兼具可解释与跨模型泛化能力；代码与数据已开源（CounterVHD）。

Abstract: Large vision-language models (LVLMs) are increasingly used for clinical image understanding, yet they remain vulnerable to \emph{hallucinations}--producing textual findings or attributes not supported by the image. We present a vision-traceable hallucination detection framework that audits arbitrary LVLM responses via visual evidence grounding, requiring neither modification nor internal access to the hidden states of LVLMs. Given an LVLM response, we extract visually verifiable entities and use a medical-domain-adapted Qwen-VL grounding verifier to localize each entity on the input image. To enhance the robustness of our detection method, we introduce a counterfactual entity perturbation method and estimate visual evidence uncertainty by contrasting factual and counterfactual grounding results. Specifically, we compute an entity-level uncertainty score from the positive confidence, counterfactual confidence, and their grounding overlap for binary hallucination decision-making. Experiments on multiple medical imaging modalities and LVLM backbones demonstrate that our method consistently improves hallucination detection performance over recent baselines, while providing interpretable localization evidence and strong cross-model transferability. Code and dataset are available at https://github.com/Agentic-CliniAI/CounterVHD.

### [26] [MammoFlow: Multiview Mammogram Synthesis with Anatomically Consistent Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28537)
*Yuexi Du,Leya Barrientos,Laura Sheiman,John Lewin,Hemant D. Tagare,Nicha C. Dvornek*

Main category: cs.CV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多视角乳腺摄影需要成对CC/MLO视图以实现三维定位，但真实配对高质量数据难以获取且不平衡，限制了深度学习训练与泛化。需要一种既能保持物理合理性又能生成成对图像的数据合成方法。

Method: 基于CC与MLO视图的固有几何关系：1) 设计对齐模块，在2D仿射变换子空间中搜索最优解以建立解剖对应；2) 在对齐后，引入像素空间的自一致性损失——沿前后(AP)轴的1D组织分布之间的EMD(地球移动距离)；3) 将上述先验集成到预训练的flow matching生成模型中，使生成的CC/MLO对在胸壁到乳头方向共享合理的组织分布。

Result: 生成图像质量优于基线，通过放射科医生主观评估；合成的多视角配对在组织分布上更一致；用于下游分类任务可将AUC提升约5%。开源代码已提供。

Conclusion: 通过隐式几何/组织对应先验与EMD自一致性约束，MammoFlow能合成物理一致的CC/MLO成对乳腺片，改善数据稀缺问题并提升下游性能，展示了将几何约束融入生成模型的有效性。

Abstract: Multiview mammography relies on paired craniocaudal (CC) and mediolateral oblique (MLO) views to provide complementary projections of a 3D breast volume, enabling precise anomaly localization. However, acquiring high-quality, balanced datasets remains challenging for deep learning applications. We propose a novel method to synthesize multiview mammograms by leveraging the inherent geometric relationship between CC and MLO views. To enforce an implicit 3D consistency prior during generation, we develop an alignment module that searches a 2D affine transformation subspace to establish optimal anatomical correspondence. Leveraging this alignment, we introduce a pixel-space self-consistency loss based on the Earth Mover's Distance (EMD) between the 1D anteroposterior (AP) axis tissue distributions of the generated images. Integrated into a pretrained flow matching model, MammoFlow forces synthesized pairs to share physically plausible tissue distributions from the chest wall to the nipple. To our knowledge, this is the first work to guide multiview mammogram generation using implicit geometric tissue correspondence. Our method demonstrates superior image quality, passes expert radiologist evaluation, and generates physically consistent pairs that improve downstream classification AUC by 5%. Code is available at https://github.com/XYPB/MammoFlow

Abstract: Building performant Vision-Language Models (VLMs) requires carefully curating large-scale training datasets, yet the community lacks systematic benchmarks for evaluating such curation strategies. We introduce DataComp for VLMs (DCVLM), a benchmark for controlled data-centric experiments to improve VLM training. As part of DCVLM, we collect 160 datasets spanning four data types -- image-caption pairs, multimodal interleaved documents, text-only, and instruction-tuning data -- into a corpus of 6T multimodal tokens. DCVLM allows participants to test curation strategies (filtering, mixing, formatting, sampling) across 1B-8B models and 6.25B-200B token budgets. Models are then evaluated on a carefully selected suite of up to 52 downstream benchmarks across 9 domains. We conduct extensive experiments on DCVLM and find that data mixing, not filtering, is key to a high-quality training dataset: instruction-heavy mixtures scale better than caption-heavy ones, with gains widening at larger scales. The resulting dataset, DCVLM-Baseline, enables training an 8B VLM to 63.6% accuracy on our 33-task core suite with 200B training tokens. Compared to FineVision, the state-of-the-art open VLM training dataset, this represents an improvement of +5.4pp. DCVLM and all accompanying artifacts will be made publicly available at https://www.datacomp.ai/dcvlm/.

Abstract: Athlete assessment is a critical process for tracking physical progress and identifying elite talent. To overcome the latency and token constraints associated with multimodal video processing, we introduce a 3 X 3 "Smart Grid" temporal chunking strategy, reducing computational overhead by over 88% while preserving critical temporal continuity. To ensure data integrity and mitigate hallucination, the framework pioneers an autonomous "LLM-as-a-Judge" self-correction loop that cross-references quantitative and qualitative metrics before persistence. Finally, we implement a dual-persistence Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) pipeline utilizing a vector search engine (ChromaDB). ### [30] [SatSplat: Geometrically-Accurate Gaussian Splatting for Satellite Imagery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28581)
*Shuang Song,Jiyong Kim,Rongjun Qin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SatSplat将2D高斯点绘适配到卫星摄影测量，通过仿射相机近似与在线相机微调、结合阴影映射与按相机颜色校正，实现在多时相、弱基线条件下的高效高精三维重建，并在DFC2019与IARPA2016上显著优于3DGS基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高分辨率卫星影像的三维重建既需速度也需几何精度。现有把3DGS用于卫星的方案在多日期、光照变化与小交会角（高航高）条件下质量下降，限制了遥感与视觉应用，因此需要一种能适应多时相光照变化、弱几何约束且具计算高效性的重建方法。

Method: 提出SatSplat：1）以2D Gaussian Splatting为场景表示；2）用仿射相机模型近似卫星相机，并从稠密观测学习最小增量参数化进行在线相机微调；3）训练中引入几何阴影映射和按相机的颜色校正，以适应时间变化的阴影与光照差异；4）端到端优化得到高效且稳定的重建。

Result: 在DFC2019与IARPA2016基准上，SatSplat取得更强几何精度并显著超越3DGS类基线；在处理过的DFC2019数据上，相比先前SOTA，平均绝对误差降低11.93%，峰值显存降低31%，实现更大规模的数字表面模型重建。

Conclusion: 2DGS与在线相机微调相结合、并融合阴影与颜色校正，可在多时相卫星影像下实现高效、鲁棒的三维重建。SatSplat在精度与效率上均具优势，适合大规模DSM构建。

Abstract: High-resolution satellite imagery demands 3D reconstruction methods that deliver both speed and geometric accuracy. Recent adaptations of 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) to satellite imagery demonstrate strong efficiency, but reconstruction quality often degrades under diverse illumination across multi-date, high-altitude acquisitions (with small intersection angles), limiting applicability to remote sensing and vision tasks. We present SatSplat, the first framework to adapt 2D Gaussian Splatting (2DGS) to satellite photogrammetry, with online camera adjustment. We approximate satellite cameras with an affine model and learn a minimal delta parameterization for in-splat camera refinement from dense observations. The formulation is implemented with a 2DGS scene representation. To handle time-varying shadows and illumination changes, we integrate geometric shadow mapping and per-camera color correction during training. Across the evaluated DFC2019 and IARPA2016 benchmark sites, SatSplat achieves strong geometric accuracy while significantly outperforming prior 3DGS-based baselines. On our processed DFC2019 benchmark, SatSplat reduces mean absolute error by 11.93% and peak video memory by 31% relative to the previous state of the art. Our approach enables large-scale digital surface modeling with practical computational efficiency. The project page is available at https://gdaosu.github.io/satsplat/.

### [32] [IMU-HOI: A Symbiotic Framework for Coherent Human-Object Interaction and Motion Capture via Contact-Conscious Inertial Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28604)
*Lizhou Lin,Songpengcheng Xia,Zengyuan Lai,Lan Sun,Jiarui Yang,Ling Pei*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从人体与物体的IMU流中直接估计手-物接触概率，以此在运动学与惯性推理间进行“路由”。基于该高层接触线索，设计三阶段融合：逐步细化人体姿态与根部平移；物体运动由手部前向运动学与物体IMU积分进行融合，从而获得一致、抗漂移的人体与物体轨迹。框架可无缝接入现有稀疏IMU动捕主干。

Result: 在具有挑战的人-物交互场景上，相比现有惯性动捕方法显著提升人体姿态与物体轨迹的精度与稳定性，并有效降低漂移。

Conclusion: IMU-HOI将纯惯性动捕从“孤立人体”扩展到“人-物联动”与联合运动估计，且易集成至现有稀疏IMU系统，为AR/VR与机器人应用提供更可靠的人物与物体联合轨迹恢复。

Abstract: Capturing full-body human motion with object interactions is crucial for AR/VR and robotics applications, yet it remains challenging for conventional vision-based methods due to occlusions and constrained capture volumes. Inertial measurement units (IMUs) offer a compelling alternative without line-of-sight requirements, but existing IMU-based motion capture assumes an isolated human and ignores object contacts and dynamics. To bridge this gap, we present IMU-HOI, a novel framework that jointly recovers full-body human pose and 6-DoF object trajectory from sparse IMUs on the body and object, explicitly modeling human-object interaction. Our approach first infers probabilistic hand-object contacts directly from IMU streams and uses them as a high-level signal to route between kinematic and inertial reasoning. These contact cues drive a three-stage fusion pipeline that refines human pose and root translation, and fuses hand-based forward kinematics with object-IMU integration for object motion, yielding coherent, drift-resilient trajectories for both human and object. Experiments on challenging human-object interaction scenarios demonstrate substantial accuracy gains over prior inertial motion capture methods. Moreover, IMU-HOI can be plugged into existing sparse-IMU mocap backbones with minimal changes, effectively extending the scope of purely inertial motion capture from isolated humans to full human-object interaction and joint motion estimation.

### [33] [Meshtryoshka: Differentiable Rendering of Real-World Scenes via Mesh Rasterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28622)
*David Charatan,Daniel Xu,Richard Szeliski,George Kopanas,Vincent Sitzmann*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Meshtryoshka：用嵌套网格壳与现成三角形光栅器实现可微渲染，适用于大规模无界场景，重建与新视角合成效果接近SOTA非网格方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主流可微渲染常依赖特殊表示与定制渲染器，而图形学下游多依赖三角网格；既有基于网格的方法难以处理大尺度无界场景。需要一种既使用网格与通用渲染工具、又能在复杂场景中达到高质量的新方法。

Method: 提出由多层“套娃式”嵌套网格壳组成的3D表示：每次前向从SDF等值面提取各层网格；为顶点计算基于符号距离的透明度；各网格独立用现成三角形光栅器光栅化，最终通过alpha合成成像。关键是仅通过透明度梯度回传到SDF，间接更新网格顶点位置，从而无需对顶点位置可微的专用渲染器。

Result: 在物体中心场景上性能与基于表面的可微渲染技术相当；在无界、真实3D场景中实现高质量新视角合成，接近SOTA的非网格方法，同时保持网格友好特性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 利用常规图形学工具（标准光栅器+网格）即可有效解决可微渲染问题；Meshtryoshka展示了网格可微渲染在大规模场景中的可行性，为面向网格的下游任务提供高质量重建/合成管线。

Abstract: Differentiable rendering has emerged as a powerful approach for 3D reconstruction and novel view synthesis. State-of-the-art differentiable rendering methods combine a variety of custom representations of 3D geometry and appearance with specialized renderers. However, most downstream tasks in computer graphics rely on 3D meshes. While prior work has attempted differentiable rendering with mesh representations, these approaches are limited to object-centric scenes and fail to reconstruct large-scale, unbounded scenes. In this work, we introduce Meshtryoshka, a novel mesh differentiable rendering framework that combines an off-the-shelf triangle rasterizer with a 3D representation that consists of nested mesh shells which resemble a matryoshka doll. In every forward pass, the mesh shells are extracted anew from a 3D signed distance function via iso-surface extraction, and the opacities for each vertex are computed as a function of signed distance. Each mesh shell is then rasterized independently, and the final image is created via alpha compositing. Crucially, mesh vertex positions are updated only indirectly via gradients that flow through the opacity values into the signed distance function, and hence, our method is compatible with off-the-shelf mesh renderers that need not be differentiable with respect to vertex positions. On object-centric scenes, our method performs competitively with surface-based differentiable rendering techniques. Our differentiable mesh rendering method scales to unbounded, real-world 3D scenes, where it yields high-quality novel view synthesis results approaching those of state-of-the-art, non-mesh methods. Our method suggests that it may be possible to solve the differentiable rendering problem without relying on specialized renderers, only using conventional tools from the computer graphics toolbox.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Physics-grounded Disentangled Flow (PDF)。利用两套flow matching网络：1) 形态演化流，学习病灶形变与生长；2) 强度演化流，学习由病灶浓度变化驱动的信号变化。为形态流加入基于病灶生长动力学的PDE正则（扩散-反应-平流方程），以物理约束指导学习。

Abstract: Forecasting longitudinal brain lesion evolution is critical for disease monitoring and treatment planning. Existing approaches typically learn a direct mapping from a baseline image to a future observation, without explicitly modeling the physical mechanisms underlying the lesion progression. Such an entangled modeling of structural deformation and image intensity variation limits physical plausibility, model generalization, and interpretability. To address this, we propose PDF, a Physics-grounded Disentangled Flow matching framework for longitudinal brain disease forecasting. We explicitly decompose the longitudinal modeling of lesion growth into two processes, each learned by a dedicated flow matching network: morphology evolution, which captures lesion growth and structural deformation; and intensity evolution, which models signal changes driven by variations in lesion concentration. To enforce physics-grounded constraints, we introduce a PDE-regularized loss based on lesion growth dynamics, that enforces a diffusion-reaction-advection formulation for morphological evolution. Experiments on three public longitudinal datasets spanning diverse brain diseases demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, validating the effectiveness of the disentangled modeling framework and physics-grounded learning design. Code is publicly available at https://github.com/jhuldr/PDF.

Abstract: Inverse rendering requires separating illumination from surface materials, which is highly ambiguous due to their tight coupling in observed images. While Gaussian Splatting is efficient for novel view synthesis, existing relightable methods approximate scene lighting using discrete point lights, global environment maps, or implicit representations. By ignoring the physical spatial extent of real-world emitters, these approaches produce incorrect light attenuation and unrealistic shadows. We present AEGIR (Area Emitters for Gaussian Inverse Rendering), a framework that explicitly models local area emitters within a relightable Gaussian Splatting representation. Joint optimization of emitters, materials, and geometry is challenging due to flexible emitter parameterization, which increases both the number of parameters and the ambiguity between illumination and materials. We address this by introducing a differentiable deferred rendering pipeline that integrates multiple importance sampling with targeted regularization. As a result, AEGIR accurately simulates local light transport and achieves more consistent decomposition. Method: Obliviate为基于指导的擦除框架，三大设计：1) 基于KL散度的监督，对视觉token分布施加约束；2) 采用整段自回归轨迹级更新，覆盖完整rollout而非单步；3) 使用对齐的视觉前缀（visual prefixes）以构造稳定的目标信号。

Abstract: The widespread adoption of generative AI models has intensified concerns about misuse, including the creation of unsafe or disturbing imagery. To mitigate such issues, several concept erasure approaches have been proposed to remove harmful content from multimodal generative models. Yet concept erasure for autoregressive image generation remains largely unexplored, despite the growing relevance of these models in recent trends toward unified multimodal architectures. In this work, we fill this gap by introducing Obliviate, a guidance-based concept erasure method for autoregressive image generation. Our method builds on three key design choices: KL-based supervision over visual token distributions, trajectory-level updates over full autoregressive rollouts, and aligned visual prefixes for stable target construction. ### [38] [FedLAS: Feature-Modulated Bidirectional Label Smoothing for Neural Network Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28654)
*Thiru Thillai Nadarasar Bahavan,Sachith Seneviratne,Saman Halgamuge*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FedLAS：一种特征调制的双向标签平滑方法，通过样本级置信状态识别与动态平滑，同时缓解过度自信与不足自信，显著提升DNN校准（降低ECE/Adaptive ECE）且不损失Top-1精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统标签平滑及其变体（如MbLS）使用预设、统一的平滑策略，仅面向过度自信问题，忽视样本难度与模型训练动态；现实中样本会随训练阶段呈现过/不足自信并存，需要能按样本、按步次自适应地确定平滑强度与方向的机制。

Method: 提出FedLAS，可插拔地嵌入基于LS/MbLS的损失中：1) 以特征范数构造置信指示器NCI，用于调节每个样本的平滑强度；2) 设计双向校准门控BCG，检测并分别处理过度自信与不足自信，从而进行双向（增加或减少熵）的标签平滑；在标准DNN上训练时逐步对每样本进行动态调整。

Result: 在标准与细粒度高分辨率视觉基准上，FedLAS相较现代基线持续降低ECE与自适应ECE，同时维持Top-1准确率；代码已开源。

Conclusion: 样本级、特征驱动且双向的动态标签平滑能更好匹配样本与训练动态，较统一的单向LS/MbLS在不牺牲准确率的前提下显著改进模型校准，可作为现有LS类损失的通用增强模块。

Abstract: Deep Neural Network (DNN) classifiers suffer from poor calibration when their softmax outputs (predictive confidence) deviate from the empirical likelihoods. This manifests itself as either overconfident incorrect predictions or under-confident correct predictions. Label smoothing (LS) enhances model calibration by introducing entropy regularization during training through redistributing probability mass from the ground-truth label to the remaining classes. LS, including Margin-based LS (MbLS), have restrictive assumptions: they rely on predefined, uniform smoothing rules and only tackle overconfidence. In reality, samples exhibit diverse characteristics, such as difficulty/ambiguity, that interact with the evolving nature of the model being trained. In training, samples may have various degrees of under- or overconfidence. To overcome this, a mechanism that identifies the specific confidence state of each sample and determines the appropriate degree of smoothing in each training step is needed, tailoring the adjustment to the individual sample. We propose FedLAS: Feature-Modulated Bidirectional Label Smoothing, a plug-and-play algorithm for label smoothing-based losses. In FedLAS, we introduce a Feature Norm-based Confidence Indicator (NCI) to control smoothing and a Bidirectional Calibration Gating (BCG) module to detect both over and under-confidence. Our algorithm can be integrated with LS and MbLS based losses when applied to standard DNNs, enhancing performance. Extensive experiments on standard and fine-grained high-resolution vision benchmarks show that FedLAS consistently improves calibration compared to modern baselines, reducing Expected Calibration Error (ECE) and Adaptive ECE while maintaining Top-1 accuracy. Code: github.com/nadarasarbahavan/FEDLAS

</details>


### [39] [SemDynReg: Semantics-Guided Deformation Regularization for Dynamic 3D Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28656)
*Ruitao Chen,Mozhang Guo,Jinge Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种语义引导的动态正则化框架，提升动态3D高斯喷溅在对象层面的变形一致性，从而在渲染质量上优于基线。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于变形场的动态3DGS方法缺乏显式对象级建模，导致同一对象内部的高斯变形不一致及不同对象间的不必要耦合，影响渲染稳定性与质量。

Method: 利用SAM获取分割掩码，并从图像提取语义特征；通过与预定义对象字典的特征相关性匹配生成object-ID图；在此引导下，为每个对象选取像素级top-k贡献高斯，并在其变形参数（位置、尺度、旋转）上施加一致性正则化，以实现对象级语义约束的变形学习。

Result: 在动态3DGS渲染任务上，相比无对象级约束的基线方法，取得更高PSNR与SSIM、更低LPIPS，表现出更一致的对象级变形。

Conclusion: 语义感知的对象级正则化能有效缓解高斯变形的内部不一致与跨对象耦合问题，提升动态场景渲染质量；为将语义先验融入动态3D表示提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Deformable 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has emerged as an efficient approach for rendering dynamic scenes in a wide range of 3D applications. However, existing deformation field-based approaches largely lack explicit object-level modeling, often resulting in inconsistent Gaussian deformations within individual objects and unwanted coupling between different objects. To address this limitation, we introduce a semantics-guided framework that enforces dynamic regularization at the object level, aiming to achieve spatially consistent object-wise deformation. Specifically, we first extract segmentation masks using the Segment Anything Model (SAM) and derive semantic features from input images. An object-ID map is then constructed via feature relevance matching with a predefined object dictionary. Guided by this object-ID map, we identify the pixel-wise top-k contributing Gaussians for each object and impose consistency regularization on their deformation parameters, including position, scale, and rotation. Unlike prior methods that learn deformation fields without explicit object-level constraints, our approach incorporates semantic cues to guide deformation behavior at the object level. Experimental results demonstrate that our semantics-aware regularization improves object-level deformation consistency and outperforms baseline methods in rendering quality, achieving higher PSNR and SSIM and lower LPIPS in dynamic 3DGS rendering. Our project page is available at https://dyn-reg-3dgs.github.io/.

</details>

Abstract: Sign Languages (SLs) are the primary means of communication for millions of deaf individuals, yet existing evaluation metrics for generated SL remain simplistic and poorly aligned with human judgements. We introduce BackTranslation2.0, a linguistically grounded evaluation metric for text-to-sign translation that moves beyond naïve backtranslation. Our approach adopts an agentic framework in which a deterministic pipeline orchestrates a suite of specialised tools to assess four scoring dimensions - grammatical correctness, phonological accuracy, motion fluency, and generation fidelity - aligned with human rater assessments. Tool outputs are not treated independently: a set of large language model (LLM)-based cross-referential comparison modules evaluates consistency across tools and checks outputs against linguistic expectations, enabling structured reasoning over grammatical, phonological, and motion-level evidence. Final dimension scores are computed through deterministic weighted formulas over validated tool outputs. To validate BackTranslation2.0, we introduce and evaluate on a British Sign Language (BSL) dataset rated in a human rater study across the same quality dimensions, following a protocol developed in collaboration between linguists and deaf experts, benchmarking against six baseline metrics. Our method demonstrates strong correlation with human judgements across all dimensions, providing a more comprehensive, interpretable, and linguistically principled evaluation framework for sign language production systems.

### [42] [SATB-VR: Training Few-Step Video Restoration Diffusion Model using SNR-Aware Trajectory Blending](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28677)
*Haoran Bai,Xiaoxu Chen,Xiaoyu Liu,Zongsheng Yue,Sibin Deng,Wangmeng Zuo,Ying Chen*

TL;DR: 提出SATB-VR：用少量步数进行视频修复，通过辅助预测器跳过早期低SNR去噪步骤，并用SNR感知的轨迹混合与一致性损失解决训练-推理偏差，实现≤5步下优于现有方法的画质与效率平衡。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 设计少步范式SATB-VR：引入辅助预测器先行预测中/后期状态，直接跳过早期低SNR去噪步骤，再接入去噪器完成重建。2) 提出SNR-Aware Trajectory Blending（SATB）：在前向生成噪声输入时，依据SNR动态混合预测器输出与真实轨迹，迫使去噪器能纠正预测误差并平滑收敛到干净数据流形。3) 提出Denoiser-Driven Consistency（DDC）损失：用同步更新的去噪器作为动态评估器，对齐内部特征与输出，提高预测器精度。
